     def init_muse(self):

         use_nconfig = self.args_data.get('use_nconfig', False)

         if not use_nconfig:
             local_cfg = self._load_local_config()
             if local_cfg is not None:
                 self.muse_lib = local_cfg.get('muse_lib', 'h55')
                 self.muse_user = local_cfg.get('muse_user', self.user_mail)
                 self.muse_asset_type = local_cfg.get('muse_asset_type', 'simpleaction')
                 self.force_update = local_cfg.get('force_update', False)
                 self.force_update_file = local_cfg.get('force_update_file', False)
                 self.asset_name_max = local_cfg.get('asset_name_max', 0)
                 self.sync_ext = local_cfg.get('sync_ext', 'max')
                 self.category_root = local_cfg.get('category_root')
                 self.category_start = local_cfg.get('category_start', 0)
                 self.category_end = local_cfg.get('category_end', -1)
                 self.asset_name_index = local_cfg.get('asset_name_index', 0)
                 self.default_asset_name = local_cfg.get('default_asset_name', '')
                 self.security_level = local_cfg.get('security_level', 'ip')
                 self.sync_ext_source = 'local_yaml'
                 lprint(f'[init_muse] 使用本地配置: {local_cfg.get("source")}')
             else:
                 lprint(f'[init_muse] 本地配置未命中，回退到 nconfig')
                 self._init_muse_from_nconfig()
                 self.sync_ext_source = 'nconfig_fallback'
         else:
             self._init_muse_from_nconfig()
             self.sync_ext_source = 'nconfig'

         # 命令行传入的 force_update 优先级最高
         if 'force_update' in self.args_data:
             self.force_update = self.args_data['force_update']

         lprint(f'[init_muse] lib={self.muse_lib} asset_type={self.muse_asset_type} user={self.muse_user} force_update={self.force_update} sync_ext={self.sync_ext!r}')
         lprint(f'[init_muse] category_root={self.category_root}')

         self.muse = muse_python_api.MuseClient(
             self.muse_user, self.muse_lib,
             getattr(MuseAssetType, self.muse_asset_type))

         lprint(f'[init_muse] 最终 sync_ext 来源={self.sync_ext_source} 值={self.sync_ext!r}')
         # 初始化 MuseHelper（复用 muse）；上传并发不由此处 max_concurrent 决定，见 run_parallel 中 batch_upload(max_workers=…)
         lprint.trace_start(auto_result=True)  # 💡 use_nconfig=False (bool)  # 💡 [[EXPAND:var_expand_2453355161488_168:local_cfg=dict (local_cfg), 340 字符（点击展开）]]
         self.muse_helper = MuseHelper(  # → 调用 __init__()
             user_email=self.muse_user,
             organization_id=self.muse_lib,
             asset_type=self.muse_asset_type,
             timeout=60.0,
             muse_client=self.muse  # 传入已初始化的 MuseClient 实例
         )
         lprint(f'[init_muse] MuseHelper 初始化完成（复用现有 MuseClient）')  # ⬅️ (第297行) None

     @beartype  # 💡 self=<anim_upload_muse_tool.muse_helper.main.MuseHelper object at 0x00000232C29F0F90>, user_email='wb.fengqingqing@mesg.corp.netease.com', organization_id='h55', asset_type='simpleaction', muse_url='https://muse.gz.netease.com', security_level='internal', max_concurrent=5, timeout=60.0, limit_per_category=10000, cache_dir=None, muse_client=<muse_python_api.main.MuseClient object at 0x00000232C14E38D0>
     def __init__(
         self,
         user_email: str,
         organization_id: Optional[str] = None,
         asset_type: Optional[str] = None,
         muse_url: str = "https://muse.gz.netease.com",
         security_level: str = "internal",
         max_concurrent: int = 5,
         timeout: float = 60.0,
         limit_per_category: int = 10000,
         cache_dir: Optional[str] = None,
         muse_client: Optional[MuseClient] = None
     ) -> None:
         """
         初始化 MuseHelper

         Args:
             user_email: 用户邮箱
             organization_id: 组织ID（资产库代码，如 'h72'）
             asset_type: 资产类型（如 'simpleaction'）
             muse_url: Muse 服务地址
             security_level: 安全级别 (internal/secret/public)
             max_concurrent: 最大并发数
             timeout: 单个任务超时时间（秒）
             limit_per_category: 批量查询时每个分类的默认资产数量限制
             cache_dir: 分类树缓存目录（如果不指定则使用用户主目录）
             muse_client: 可选的已初始化 MuseClient 实例（如果提供则复用，否则创建新的）
         """
         self.muse_url = muse_url  # 💡 self.muse_url='https://muse.gz.netease.com' (str)
         self.user_email = user_email  # 💡 self.user_email='wb.fengqingqing@mesg.corp.netease.com' (str)
         self.organization_id = organization_id  # 💡 self.organization_id='h55' (str)
         self.asset_type = asset_type  # 💡 self.asset_type='simpleaction' (str)
         self.security_level = security_level  # 💡 self.security_level='internal' (str)
         self.limit_per_category = limit_per_category  # 💡 self.limit_per_category=10000 (int)
         self.cache_dir = cache_dir

         # 如果提供了外部客户端，直接使用；否则创建新的
         if muse_client is not None:
             self.muse_client = muse_client  # 💡 self.muse_client=<muse_python_api.main.MuseClient object at 0x00000232C14E38D0> (MuseClient)
             lprint(f'[MuseHelper] 使用外部传入的 MuseClient 实例')
         else:
             self.muse_client = MuseClient(
                 email=user_email,
                 organization_id=organization_id,
                 asset_type=asset_type
             )
             lprint(f'[MuseHelper] 创建新的 MuseClient 实例')

         # 将 limit_per_category 添加到 muse_client，供服务层使用
         self.muse_client.limit_per_category = limit_per_category

         # 初始化服务层
         self.asset_service = AssetService(
             self.muse_client, 
             organization_id, 
             asset_type,
             max_concurrent,
             timeout
         )
         self.category_service = CategoryService(
             self.muse_client,
             organization_id,
             asset_type,
             cache_dir=cache_dir,
             max_concurrent=max_concurrent,
             timeout=timeout
         )
         self.upload_service = UploadService(
             self.muse_client,
             organization_id,
             asset_type,
             max_concurrent,
             timeout
         )
         self.tag_service = TagService(  # → 调用 __init__()  # ⬅️ (第177行) None
             self.muse_client,
             self.asset_service,
             self.category_service,
             organization_id,
             asset_type,
             max_concurrent,
             timeout
         )

     def run_parallel(self, max_concurrent=5):  # 💡 max_concurrent=50
         """使用 BatchUploader 并行上传文件"""
         self.load_upload_log()

         # 收集成功上传的路径（由 on_progress 填充，主线程统一写入）
         uploaded_paths = []

         # 如果 skip_p4v，直接扫描本地文件而不调用 update_p4v
         local_file_map = {}  # 本地路径到P4路径的映射

         if self.skip_p4v:
             file_list = []  # 💡 file_list=[] (list)
             local_dir = self.upload_dir.replace('\\', '/')  # 💡 local_dir='D:/PTrack/hangzhou/H55项目美术资源/角色动作资源（2025）/已有资源库' (str)
             if local_dir.startswith('//'):
                 local_dir = local_dir.replace('//hangzhou/', 'D:/PTrack/hangzhou/')

             if not os.path.exists(local_dir):
                 self.log.error(f'本地目录不存在: {local_dir}')
                 return

             scan_count = [0]  # 💡 scan_count=[0] (list)
             skip_count = [0]  # 💡 skip_count=[0] (list)
             start_time = time.time()  # 💡 start_time=1775646313.5848246 (float)
             last_print_time = [start_time]  # 💡 last_print_time=[1775646313.5848246] (list)
             limit = self.limit  # 💡 limit=1 (int)
             reached_limit = [False]

             def _scan(dir_path):
                 if reached_limit[0]:
                     return
                 try:
                     entries = list(os.scandir(dir_path))
                 except PermissionError:
                     return
                 for entry in entries:
                     if reached_limit[0]:
                         return
                     if entry.is_dir(follow_symlinks=False):
                         _scan(entry.path)
                     elif entry.is_file(follow_symlinks=False):
                         local_path = entry.path.replace('\\', '/')
                         p4_path = local_path.replace('D:/PTrack/hangzhou/', '//hangzhou/')
                         if self.is_ignore_file(p4_path):
                             skip_count[0] += 1
                             continue
                         if p4_path in self.upload_file_list:
                             skip_count[0] += 1
                             continue
                         if self.sync_ext and not p4_path.endswith(self.sync_ext):
                             skip_count[0] += 1
                             continue
                         file_list.append(p4_path)
                         self.p4v_file_list[local_path] = p4_path
                         local_file_map[p4_path] = local_path
                         scan_count[0] += 1
                         now = time.time()
                         if now - last_print_time[0] >= 5.0:
                             last_print_time[0] = now
                             lprint(f'[扫描进度] 已收集: {scan_count[0]}, 已跳过: {skip_count[0]}, 已用时: {now - start_time:.1f}秒')
                         if limit and scan_count[0] >= limit:
                             lprint(f'[扫描] 已达到 limit={limit}，提前终止')
                             reached_limit[0] = True
                             return

             _scan(local_dir)
             lprint(f'[扫描完成] 收集: {scan_count[0]}, 跳过: {skip_count[0]}, 耗时: {time.time() - start_time:.1f}秒')
         else:
             file_list = self.update_p4v()

         self.clear_files = []

         # 过滤需要上传的文件
         files_to_upload = []  # 💡 files_to_upload=[] (list)
         ignored_count = 0  # 💡 ignored_count=0 (int)
         uploaded_count = 0  # 💡 uploaded_count=0 (int)
         ext_filtered_count = 0

         lprint(f'过滤文件: 总计 {len(file_list)}, 历史记录 {len(self.upload_file_list)}')

         for file_path in file_list:
             if self.is_ignore_file(file_path):
                 ignored_count += 1
                 continue
             if file_path in self.upload_file_list:
                 uploaded_count += 1
                 self.log.debug(f'已上传过，跳过: {file_path}')
                 continue
             if self.sync_ext and not file_path.endswith(self.sync_ext):
                 ext_filtered_count += 1
                 continue
             files_to_upload.append(file_path)

         lprint(f'过滤结果: 忽略 {ignored_count}, 已上传 {uploaded_count}, 扩展名不匹配 {ext_filtered_count}, 待上传 {len(files_to_upload)}')

         # limit：只取前 N 个
         if self.limit and len(files_to_upload) > self.limit:
             lprint(f'[limit] 限制上传数量: {self.limit} / {len(files_to_upload)}')
             files_to_upload = files_to_upload[:self.limit]

         if not files_to_upload:
             lprint('没有需要上传的文件')
             self.clear_disk_files()
             return

         # dry_run：与服务器对比标签，不实际上传
         if self.dry_run:
             lprint(f'[dry_run] 以下 {len(files_to_upload)} 个文件将被上传（dry_run 模式，不实际执行）, 标签规则共 {len(self.tag_rules)} 条')

             # 预先缓存分类树，避免在循环中重复调用API
             lprint(f'[缓存] 正在获取分类树...')
             self._cached_organization_dir = self.muse.get_organization_dir()  # 💡 self._cached_organization_dir={...2 keys} (dict)
             lprint(f'[缓存] 分类树已缓存')

             # 递归收集所有子分类ID
             all_category_ids = []  # 💡 all_category_ids=[] (list)
             if self.muse_category_path:
                 target_category_path = [p.strip() for p in self.muse_category_path.split('/')]  # 💡 target_category_path=['H55动画', '动作库', '已有资源库'] (list)
                 lprint(f'[查询根路径] {" / ".join(target_category_path)}')
                 category_id_chain = self.muse_helper.category_service.get_category_ids_by_path(
                     target_category_path, recursive=False, full_chain=True, use_cache=True
                 )
                 if category_id_chain:
                     all_category_ids = [category_id_chain[-1]]
                     lprint(f'[分类收集] 目标分类: {" / ".join(target_category_path)} (ID: {all_category_ids[0]})')
                 else:
                     lprint(f'[分类收集] 未找到目标分类节点: {target_category_path}')
             else:
                 lprint(f'[错误] 未设置 muse_category_path 参数，无法进行 dry-run 查询')

             # 批量获取所有分类的资产数据
             category_assets_map = {}
             if all_category_ids:
                 try:
                     lprint(f'\n[批量查询] 正在获取 {len(all_category_ids)} 个分类的资产数据...')
                     category_assets_map = self._fetch_category_assets_map(all_category_ids)
                     total_assets = sum(len(assets) for assets in category_assets_map.values())
                     lprint(f'[批量查询] 完成，共获取 {total_assets} 个资产')
                 except Exception as e:
                     lprint(f'[批量查询] 失败: {e}')
                     traceback.print_exc()

             # 收集所有文件信息并计算新标签
             lprint(f'\n[解析] 正在解析 {len(files_to_upload)} 个文件...')
             asset_info_list = []
             for fp in files_to_upload:
                 try:
                     asset_name, category_list = self.get_name_category(fp)
                     path_parts = category_list[len(self.category_root or []):]
                     new_tags, tag_key = self._get_tags_for_path(self.tag_rules, path_parts)
                     asset_info_list.append({
                         'file_path': fp,
                         'asset_name': asset_name,
                         'category_list': category_list,
                         'path_parts': path_parts,
                         'new_tags': new_tags,
                         'tag_key': tag_key
                     })
                 except Exception as e:
                     lprint(f'  {fp}  (解析失败: {e})')
             lprint(f'[解析] 完成，共解析 {len(asset_info_list)} 个文件')

             # 匹配并输出结果
             lprint(f'\n{"="*80}')
             processed_count = 0

             # 构建分类ID→名称映射
             category_id_to_name = {}
             def _collect_id_name(nodes):
                 for node in nodes:
                     nid = str(node.get('id', ''))
                     name = node.get('name_multil', {}).get('zh_CN', '')
                     if nid:
                         category_id_to_name[nid] = name
                     _collect_id_name(node.get('children', []))
             _collect_id_name(self._cached_organization_dir.get(self.muse_lib, []))

             for info in asset_info_list:
                 old_tags = None
                 asset_id = None
                 local_category_str = ' > '.join(info['category_list']).lower()
                 for category_key, assets_list in category_assets_map.items():
                     for asset in assets_list:
                         if asset.asset_name == info['asset_name']:
                             if asset.category_names:
                                 if isinstance(asset.category_names, list):
                                     if all(str(cn).isdigit() for cn in asset.category_names):
                                         names = [category_id_to_name.get(str(cn), str(cn)) for cn in asset.category_names]
                                         server_category_str = ' > '.join(names).lower()
                                     else:
                                         server_category_str = ' > '.join(asset.category_names).lower()
                                 else:
                                     server_category_str = str(asset.category_names).lower()
                                 if local_category_str == server_category_str or \
                                    local_category_str.endswith(server_category_str) or \
                                    server_category_str.endswith(local_category_str):
                                     old_tags = asset.tags
                                     asset_id = asset.asset_id
                                     break
                             else:
                                 old_tags = asset.tags
                                 asset_id = asset.asset_id
                                 break
                     if old_tags is not None:
                         break

                 file_info = f'\n  {info["file_path"]}\n    分类: {" / ".join(info["category_list"])}\n    资产名: {info["asset_name"]}'
                 needs_update = False
                 if old_tags is not None:
                     old_set = set(old_tags) if old_tags else set()
                     new_set = set(info['new_tags']) if info['new_tags'] else set()
                     needs_update = old_set != new_set
                     tag_info = f'    ⚠️ 服务器旧标签: {old_tags} (asset_id={asset_id}) [需要更新]' if needs_update else f'    服务器旧标签: {old_tags} (asset_id={asset_id}) [标签一致]'
                 else:
                     tag_info = '    服务器旧标签: [资产不存在]'
                 if info['tag_key']:
                     update_mark = ' ⚠️' if needs_update else ''
                     local_tag_info = f'    本地新标签: key="{info["tag_key"]}" -> {info["new_tags"]}{update_mark}'
                 else:
                     local_tag_info = f'    本地新标签: 未命中规则 path_parts={info["path_parts"]}'
                 has_career_skill = any("职业技能" in cat for cat in info["category_list"])
                 if has_career_skill:
                     lprint(file_info + '\n' + tag_info + '\n' + local_tag_info)
                 elif needs_update or old_tags is None:
                     lprint(file_info + '\n' + tag_info + '\n' + local_tag_info, max_prints_per_line=10)
                 else:
                     lprint(file_info + '\n' + tag_info + '\n' + local_tag_info, max_prints_per_line=2)
                 processed_count += 1

             lprint(f'\n{"="*80}\n[统计] 总共处理了 {processed_count} 个资产\n{"="*80}')
             return  # ⬅️ (第1404行) None

         lprint(f'发现 {len(files_to_upload)} 个文件待上传，使用{max_concurrent}并发')

         # 批量预查询所有资产（避免每个文件都调用API）
         lprint(f'\n[批量查询] 正在预查询目标分类的所有资产...')
         self._debug_log('H_PREQUERY', 'prequery start', {
             'files_to_upload': len(files_to_upload),
             'muse_category_path': self.muse_category_path,
             'muse_lib': str(self.muse_lib),
         })
         self._cached_assets_map = {}
         if self.muse_category_path:
             try:
                 self._cached_organization_dir = self.muse.get_organization_dir()
                 target_category_path = [p.strip() for p in self.muse_category_path.split('/')]
                 category_id_chain = self.muse_helper.category_service.get_category_ids_by_path(
                     target_category_path, recursive=False, full_chain=True, use_cache=True
                 )
                 if category_id_chain:
                     category_id = category_id_chain[-1]
                     lprint(f'[批量查询] 目标分类: {" / ".join(target_category_path)} (ID: {category_id})')
                     self._debug_log('H_PREQUERY', 'target category resolved', {
                         'target_category_path': target_category_path,
                         'category_id': category_id,
                     })
                     self._cached_assets_map = self._load_or_rebuild_name_path_cache(category_id)
                 else:
                     lprint(f'[批量查询] 警告: 未找到目标分类节点')
                     self._debug_log('H_PREQUERY', 'target category node not found', {'target_category_path': target_category_path})
             except Exception as e:
                 lprint(f'[批量查询] 失败: {e}，将回退到逐个查询模式')
                 traceback.print_exc()
                 self._debug_log('H_PREQUERY', 'prequery exception', {'error': str(e)})
         else:
             lprint(f'[批量查询] 警告: 未设置 muse_category_path，将回退到逐个查询模式')

         # 创建上传任务列表
         tasks = []
         for fp in files_to_upload:
             local_file = local_file_map.get(fp) if self.skip_p4v else None
             tasks.append(UploadTask(
                 file_path=fp,
                 asset_name=os.path.basename(fp),
                 category_list=[],
                 metadata={'p4_path': fp, 'local_file': local_file}
             ))

         # 创建上传函数
         def upload_func(task: UploadTask) -> UploadResult:
             """单个文件上传函数"""
             try:
                 p4_path = task.metadata['p4_path']
                 local_file = task.metadata.get('local_file')
                 result = self.sync_file(p4_path, local_file)

                 # sync_file 返回 'created'/'updated'/'skipped'/'failed'
                 if result == UploadResultStatus.FAILED.value:
                     return UploadResult(
                         task=task,
                         status=UploadStatus.FAILED,
                         error_message='failed'
                     )
                 elif result == UploadResultStatus.SKIPPED.value:
                     return UploadResult(
                         task=task,
                         status=UploadStatus.SKIPPED,
                         error_message='skipped'
                     )
                 else:
                     # created / updated / recreated 都算 SUCCESS，用 error_message 保存细分状态
                     return UploadResult(
                         task=task,
                         status=UploadStatus.SUCCESS,
                         error_message=result or 'created'
                     )
             except Exception as e:
                 error_trace = traceback.format_exc()
                 error_msg = f"{type(e).__name__}: {str(e)}"
                 pipe.popo.send(f'[p4_to_muse] 文件上传失败: {task.file_path}\n{error_msg}\n{error_trace}', ERROR_NOTICE)
                 with self._report_lock:
                     with open(self._report_file, 'a', encoding='utf-8') as _f:
                         _f.write(json.dumps({
                             'action': 'failed',
                             'file_path': task.file_path,
                             'error': error_msg,
                             'traceback': error_trace,
                         }, ensure_ascii=False) + '\n')
                 return UploadResult(
                     task=task,
                     status=UploadStatus.FAILED,
                     error_message=error_msg
                 )

         # 使用 tqdm 创建进度条
         from tqdm import tqdm

         start_time = time.time()
         success_count = 0
         failed_count = 0
         detail_counts = {
             UploadResultStatus.CREATED.value: 0,
             UploadResultStatus.UPDATED.value: 0,
             UploadResultStatus.RECREATED.value: 0,
             UploadResultStatus.SKIPPED.value: 0,
             UploadResultStatus.FAILED.value: 0,
         }

         # 创建 tqdm 进度条
         pbar = tqdm(total=len(tasks), desc="上传进度", unit="文件")

         # 进度回调
         def on_progress(completed: int, total: int, result: UploadResult):
             """进度回调"""
             nonlocal success_count, failed_count

             detail_status = result.error_message or result.status.value
             if detail_status in detail_counts:
                 detail_counts[detail_status] += 1

             if result.status in (UploadStatus.SUCCESS, UploadStatus.SKIPPED):
                 success_count += 1
                 if result.task.metadata and 'p4_path' in result.task.metadata:
                     uploaded_paths.append(result.task.metadata['p4_path'])
             else:
                 failed_count += 1

             # 更新 tqdm 进度条
             pbar.set_postfix({'✓': success_count, '✗': failed_count})
             pbar.update(1)

             if result.status not in (UploadStatus.SUCCESS, UploadStatus.SKIPPED):
                 pbar.write(f'[{completed}/{total}] ✗ {result.task.file_path}: {result.error_message}')

         # 上传并发仅在此传入：CLI --max_concurrent → max_workers → UploadService.run_batch_async → Semaphore
         results = self.muse_helper.batch_upload(
             tasks=tasks,
             upload_func=upload_func,
             on_progress=on_progress,
             max_workers=max_concurrent,
         )

         # 关闭进度条
         pbar.close()

         # 统计结果（results 已经是 UploadResult 列表）
         stats = BatchUploadStats(results)
         total_time = time.time() - start_time
         avg_speed = len(tasks) / total_time if total_time > 0 else 0

         # 打印总结信息
         report = (
             f'\n{"="*80}\n上传完成！\n{"="*80}\n'
             f'总计文件: {len(tasks)} 个\n'
             f'  ✦ 新建资产: {detail_counts[UploadResultStatus.CREATED.value]} 个\n'
             f'  ✦ 更新标签: {detail_counts[UploadResultStatus.UPDATED.value]} 个\n'
             f'  ✦ 删除重建: {detail_counts[UploadResultStatus.RECREATED.value]} 个\n'
             f'  ✦ 标签匹配跳过: {detail_counts[UploadResultStatus.SKIPPED.value]} 个\n'
             f'  ✗ 失败: {detail_counts[UploadResultStatus.FAILED.value]} 个\n'
             f'总耗时: {total_time:.1f} 秒\n'
             f'平均速度: {avg_speed:.2f} 文件/秒\n'
             f'{"="*80}'
         )
         lprint(report)

         lprint(f'上传完成: 新建 {detail_counts[UploadResultStatus.CREATED.value]}, 更新标签 {detail_counts[UploadResultStatus.UPDATED.value]}, 删除重建 {detail_counts[UploadResultStatus.RECREATED.value]}, 跳过 {detail_counts[UploadResultStatus.SKIPPED.value]}, 失败 {detail_counts[UploadResultStatus.FAILED.value]}, 耗时 {total_time:.1f}秒')

         # 收集上传记录（禁用文件写入，避免文件锁超时）
         if uploaded_paths:
             for p4_path in uploaded_paths:
                 if p4_path not in self.upload_file_list:
                     self.upload_file_list.append(p4_path)
             # 禁用文件写入
             # self.log_file.save({'history': self.upload_file_list})
             lprint(f'[记录收集] 共收集 {len(uploaded_paths)} 条上传路径（未写入文件）')

         # 不删除本地文件，仅记录日志
         # self.clear_disk_files()
         lprint(f'已处理 {success_count} 个文件（新建 {detail_counts[UploadResultStatus.CREATED.value]}, 更新标签 {detail_counts[UploadResultStatus.UPDATED.value]}, 删除重建 {detail_counts[UploadResultStatus.RECREATED.value]}），本地文件已保留')

         # 写入详细检查报告到 jsonl（已增量写入，此处只打印统计）
         lprint(f'[报告] 详细检查结果已写入: {self._report_file}')
         lprint(
             f'[报告] jsonl 按任务完成顺序交错写入，非按路径排序；'
             f'本次约 skipped={detail_counts[UploadResultStatus.SKIPPED.value]} 条、'
             f'updated={detail_counts[UploadResultStatus.UPDATED.value]} 条、'
             f'created={detail_counts[UploadResultStatus.CREATED.value]} 条、'
             f'recreated={detail_counts[UploadResultStatus.RECREATED.value]} 条。'
             f'查看标签更新请在文件中搜索 "action": "updated"（或仅搜 updated）。'
         )

     def load_upload_log(self):
         # 禁用文件读取，避免文件锁超时
         self.upload_file_list = []  # ⬅️ (第1165行) None

             def _scan(dir_path):  # 💡 dir_path='D:/PTrack/hangzhou/H55项目美术资源/角色动作资源（2025）/已有资源库', file_list=[], last_print_time=[1775646313.5848246], limit=1, local_file_map={}, reached_limit=[False], scan_count=[0]
                 if reached_limit[0]:
                     return
                 try:
                     entries = list(os.scandir(dir_path))
                 except PermissionError:
                     return
                 for entry in entries:
                     if reached_limit[0]:
                         return  # ⬅️ (第1211行) None
                     if entry.is_dir(follow_symlinks=False):
                         _scan(entry.path)

     def _format_url(self, data, **kwargs):  # 💡 data=('GET', '/api/category/trees/{organization}/{asset}'), kwargs={}
         if not self.organization_id or not self.asset_type:
             raise ValueError('organization_id or asset_type is required')

         method, url = data  # 💡 method='GET' (str), url='/api/category/trees/{organization}/{asset}' (str)
         return method, url.format(  # ⬅️ (第310行) ('GET', '/api/category/trees/h55/simpleaction')
             organization=self.organization_id, asset=self.asset_type, **kwargs)

 def _patched_request(self, method, url, **kwargs):  # 💡 method='GET', url='/api/category/trees/h55/simpleaction', kwargs={}
     """打补丁的_request方法，跟踪所有API调用的耗时"""
     import threading
     import time

     start_time = time.time()  # 💡 start_time=1775646313.6255248 (float)
     stop_event = threading.Event()

     def print_progress():
         """后台线程：超过5秒后每5秒打印一次进度"""
         nonlocal start_time, method, url, kwargs

         # 先等待5秒
         if stop_event.wait(5.0):
             return  # 请求已完成

         # 第一次超过5秒，打印详细的请求信息
         info_parts = [f"[API长请求] {method} {url}"]
         if kwargs.get('params'):
             info_parts.append(f"  请求参数: {kwargs.get('params')}")
         if kwargs.get('json'):
             info_parts.append(f"  请求体: {kwargs.get('json')}")
         lprint('\n'.join(info_parts),trace_depth=10)

         # 超过5秒，开始每5秒打印进度
         while not stop_event.is_set():
             elapsed = time.time() - start_time
             lprint(f"[API请求] {method} {url} 正在处理中... 已耗时 {elapsed:.1f} 秒")
             # 再等待5秒或直到停止
             if stop_event.wait(5.0):
                 break

     # 启动后台线程
     progress_thread = threading.Thread(target=print_progress, daemon=True)  # 💡 progress_thread=<Thread(Thread-7 (print_progress), initial daemon)> (Thread)
     progress_thread.start()

     try:
         result = _original_request(self, method, url, **kwargs)
     finally:
         # 通知线程停止
         stop_event.set()
         # 等待线程结束（最多1秒）
         progress_thread.join(timeout=1.0)

     elapsed = time.time() - start_time  # 💡 elapsed=4.5071938037872314 (float)
     if elapsed > 5.0:
         lprint(f"[API请求] {method} {url} 完成，总耗时 {elapsed:.2f} 秒")

     return result  # ⬅️ [[EXPAND:ret_expand_2453355144880_1280:(第85行) {...2 keys}（点击展开）]]

     def _request(self, method, url, **kwargs):  # 💡 method='GET', url='/api/category/trees/h55/simpleaction', kwargs={}
         self._check_token()
         # category_tree
         content_type = kwargs.pop('content_type', 'application/json')
         headers = {  # 💡 content_type='application/json' (str)
             'Authorization': 'Bearer {}'.format(self._token),
             'Content-Type': content_type,
             'email': self._email,
         }


         #print ("请求url" , url)
         max_retries = 5  # 💡 max_retries=5 (int)
         base_delay = 2

         for attempt in range(max_retries):
             try:
                 response = requests.request(
                     method,
                     self._client_info.base_url + url,
                     headers=headers,
                     verify=self._verify,
                     **kwargs
                 )

                 # 如果请求成功，跳出重试循环
                 break

             except requests.exceptions.ChunkedEncodingError as e:
                 logger.warning(f'ChunkedEncodingError on attempt {attempt + 1}/{max_retries}: {e}')

                 if attempt < max_retries - 1:
                     # 指数退避策略
                     delay = base_delay * (2 ** attempt)
                     logger.info(f'Retrying in {delay} seconds...')
                     time.sleep(delay)
                     continue
                 else:
                     logger.error('Max retries exceeded for ChunkedEncodingError')
                     raise MuseError(f'Network error after {max_retries} attempts: {e}')

             except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
                 # 其他请求异常不重试，直接抛出
                 logger.error(f'Request failed with non-retryable error: {e}')
                 raise MuseError(f'Request failed: {e}')

         if response.status_code != 200:
             # lprint(url, method, kwargs,response, max_length=3800,force_print=True)
             raise MuseError(
                 'Muse API returned invalid response: {}'.format(response.text))

         try:
             result = response.json()
         except Exception as e:
             logger.error(f'Failed to parse JSON response: {e}')
             raise MuseError(
                 'Muse API returned invalid response: {}'.format(response.text))
         lprint(url, method, kwargs,result,max_prints_per_line=4, max_length=1800)
         if result['code'] != 0:
             # lprint(url, method, kwargs,result,max_prints_per_line=5, max_length=3800,force_print=True)
             raise MuseError(
                 'Muse API Response Error: {}'.format(result.get('msg', result)))
         #(url, method, kwargs,result['data'],max_prints_per_line=5, max_length=3800)
         return result['data']  # ⬅️ [[EXPAND:ret_expand_2453355145664_1357:(第146行) {...2 keys}（点击展开）]]

     def _check_token(self):

     def _get_token(self):
         try:
             encrypted_credentials = base64.b64encode(
                 CredentialUtil.encode('{}:{}'.format(
                     self._client_info.client_id,
                     self._client_info.client_secret)
                 ))
             headers = {  # 💡 [[EXPAND:var_expand_2453355192240_1383:encrypted_credentials=bytes (encrypted_credentials), 211 字符（点击展开）]]
                 'Authorization': 'Basic {}'.format(
                     CredentialUtil.decode(encrypted_credentials))
             }
             response = requests.post(
                 '{}/oauth2/token?grant_type=client_credentials&scope=all'.format(
                     self._client_info.authorization_url),
                 headers=headers,
                 verify=self._verify
             )
             if response.status_code != 200:
                 raise MuseTokenError(
                     'Could not get valid token for Muse API: {}'.format(
                         response.text
                     ))

             result = response.json()  # 💡 [[EXPAND:var_expand_2453355161056_1402:result=dict (result), 813 字符（点击展开）]]
             self._token = result.get('access_token')  # 💡 [[EXPAND:var_expand_2453355050160_1406:self._token=str (self._token), 724 字符（点击展开）]]
             self._token_expired_at = datetime.datetime.now() + datetime.timedelta(  # ⬅️ (第70行) None
                 seconds=result.get('expires_in')
             )
         except Exception as e:
             raise MuseTokenError(
                 'Could not get valid token for Muse API: {}'.format(e))

             def _scan(dir_path):  # 💡 .0=<list_iterator object at 0x00000232BFF7B190>  # ⬅️ (第1291行) ['H55动画', '动作库', '已有资源库']

                         return

                         _scan(entry.path)

                             continue
                         if p4_path in self.upload_file_list:
                             skip_count[0] += 1
                             continue
                         if self.sync_ext and not p4_path.endswith(self.sync_ext):
                             skip_count[0] += 1
                             continue
                         file_list.append(p4_path)
                         self.p4v_file_list[local_path] = p4_path
                         local_file_map[p4_path] = local_path
                         scan_count[0] += 1
                         now = time.time()
                         if now - last_print_time[0] >= 5.0:
                             last_print_time[0] = now
                             lprint(f'[扫描进度] 已收集: {scan_count[0]}, 已跳过: {skip_count[0]}, 已用时: {now - start_time:.1f}秒')

                             lprint(f'[扫描] 已达到 limit={limit}，提前终止')
                             reached_limit[0] = True
                             return

     def _get_category_list(self, use_cache: bool = True) -> Optional[List[CategoryNode]]:  # 💡 use_cache=True
         """获取当前组织的分类列表，校验树结构，失败返回 None"""
         tree = self.get_category_tree(use_cache=use_cache)  # ⬅️ (第319行) None
         if not tree:
             lprint("分类树为空（API 返回空数据）", level='WARNING')
             return None
         if self.organization_id not in tree:
             no_category_key = f"{self.organization_id}_no_category_count"
             if no_category_key in tree:
                 lprint(f"分类树为空（{self.organization_id} 下没有任何分类）", level='WARNING')
             else:
                 lprint(f"分类树响应格式异常: {list(tree.keys())}", level='ERROR')
             return None
         return tree[self.organization_id]

     def get_name_category(self, file_path):  # 💡 file_path='//hangzhou/H55项目美术资源/角色动作资源（2025）/已有资源库/个性表演/乐器表演/girl_hall_interact_cello_girl.max'
         # 统一使用 init_muse 中加载的配置参数，不再根据文件路径重新加载配置
         # 这样可以确保所有文件都使用 bat 传入的 UPLOAD_PATH 对应的统一规则

         file_path = os.path.splitext(file_path)[0].replace('\\', '/')  # 💡 file_path='//hangzhou/H55项目美术资源/角色动作资源（2025）/已有资源库/个性表演/乐器表演/girl_hall_interact_cello_girl' (str)
         file_path_items = file_path.split('/')  # 💡 file_path_items=['', '', 'hangzhou', 'H55项目美术资源', '角色动作资源（2025）', '已有资源库', '个性表演', '乐器表演', 'girl_hall_interact_cello_girl'] (list)
         asset_name = file_path_items[-1]  # 💡 asset_name='girl_hall_interact_cello_girl' (str)
         if len(file_path_items) > self.asset_name_index:
             asset_name = file_path_items[self.asset_name_index]
         elif len(file_path_items) < self.asset_name_max:
             if self.default_asset_name:
                 asset_name = self.default_asset_name
             else:
                 asset_name = file_path_items[self.category_end-1]

         # category_end 为 -1 时，自动推导为 asset_name_index（分类取资产名之前的所有层级）
         effective_category_end = self.category_end  # 💡 effective_category_end=-1 (int)
         if effective_category_end == -1 and self.asset_name_index != 0:
             effective_category_end = self.asset_name_index

         category_list = file_path_items[self.category_start:effective_category_end]

         # 优先使用 muse_category_path 参数，如果没有则使用 YAML 配置的 category_root
         if self.muse_category_path:
             category_root = [p.strip() for p in self.muse_category_path.split('/')]
             # 去除文件路径中与 muse_category_path 最后一级重复的部分
             # 例如：muse_category_path = "H55动画/动作库/已有资源库"
             #      category_list = ["已有资源库", "个性表演", "乐器表演"]
             # 结果应该是：["H55动画", "动作库", "已有资源库", "个性表演", "乐器表演"]
             if category_list and category_root and category_list[0] == category_root[-1]:
                 category_list = category_root + category_list[1:]
             else:
                 category_list = category_root + category_list
         elif self.category_root:
             category_list = self.category_root + category_list

         return asset_name, category_list  # ⬅️ (第667行) ('girl_hall_interact_cello_girl', ['H55动画', '动作库', '已有资源库', '', '', 'hangzhou', 'H55项目美术资源', '角色动作资源（2025）', '已有资源库', '个性表演', '乐器表演'])

     def get_name_category(self, file_path):  # 💡 .0=<list_iterator object at 0x00000232C1940B50>  # ⬅️ (第655行) ['H55动画', '动作库', '已有资源库']
         # 统一使用 init_muse 中加载的配置参数，不再根据文件路径重新加载配置
         # 这样可以确保所有文件都使用 bat 传入的 UPLOAD_PATH 对应的统一规则

         file_path = os.path.splitext(file_path)[0].replace('\\', '/')
         file_path_items = file_path.split('/')
         asset_name = file_path_items[-1]
         if len(file_path_items) > self.asset_name_index:
             asset_name = file_path_items[self.asset_name_index]
         elif len(file_path_items) < self.asset_name_max:
             if self.default_asset_name:
                 asset_name = self.default_asset_name
             else:
                 asset_name = file_path_items[self.category_end-1]

         # category_end 为 -1 时，自动推导为 asset_name_index（分类取资产名之前的所有层级）
         effective_category_end = self.category_end
         if effective_category_end == -1 and self.asset_name_index != 0:
             effective_category_end = self.asset_name_index

         category_list = file_path_items[self.category_start:effective_category_end]

         # 优先使用 muse_category_path 参数，如果没有则使用 YAML 配置的 category_root
         if self.muse_category_path:
             category_root = [p.strip() for p in self.muse_category_path.split('/')]
             # 去除文件路径中与 muse_category_path 最后一级重复的部分
             # 例如：muse_category_path = "H55动画/动作库/已有资源库"
             #      category_list = ["已有资源库", "个性表演", "乐器表演"]
             # 结果应该是：["H55动画", "动作库", "已有资源库", "个性表演", "乐器表演"]
             if category_list and category_root and category_list[0] == category_root[-1]:
                 category_list = category_root + category_list[1:]
             else:
                 category_list = category_root + category_list
         elif self.category_root:
             category_list = self.category_root + category_list

         return asset_name, category_list

 def get_tags_for_path(tag_rules, path_parts, separator='>'):  # 💡 tag_rules={...52 keys}, path_parts=[], separator='>'
     """
     根据 path_parts 向上追溯匹配标签规则，返回 (tags, matched_key) 元组

     匹配策略：从最长路径开始，逐级向上追溯，找到第一个匹配规则就返回。
     同时处理职业技能特殊标签逻辑。

     Args:
         tag_rules: 标签规则字典 {路径key: [标签列表]}
         path_parts: 层级路径列表，如 ['公共库资源', '战斗动作', '技能动作', '特殊技能']
         separator: 路径分隔符，默认 '>'

     Returns:
         (tags, matched_key): tags 为标签列表（未找到则为 []），matched_key 为匹配到的路径（未找到则为 None）

     示例:
         rules = {'公共库资源>战斗动作>技能动作': ['技能', '战斗', '公共']}
         path_parts = ['公共库资源', '战斗动作', '技能动作', '特殊技能']
         -> 尝试 '公共库资源>战斗动作>技能动作>特殊技能' -> 未找到
         -> 尝试 '公共库资源>战斗动作>技能动作' -> 找到！
         -> 返回 (['技能', '战斗', '公共'], '公共库资源>战斗动作>技能动作')
     """
     if not tag_rules or not path_parts:
         return [], None  # ⬅️ (第170行) ([], None)

     # 向上追溯匹配基础标签
     base_tags = []
     matched_key = None
     for end in range(len(path_parts), 0, -1):
         key = separator.join(path_parts[:end])
         if key in tag_rules:
             base_tags = list(tag_rules[key])
             matched_key = key
             break

     # 职业技能层级特殊处理
     skill_tags = []
     if '职业技能' in path_parts:
         # 找到"职业技能"的位置
         skill_index = path_parts.index('职业技能')
         # 检查职业技能后面是否有分类
         if skill_index + 1 < len(path_parts):
             # 取职业技能后的第一个分类名称作为标签
             skill_category = path_parts[skill_index + 1]
             skill_tags.append(skill_category)
             lprint(f'[职业技能] path={">".join(path_parts)}, 提取职业标签: {skill_category}')

     # 合并基础标签和职业技能标签，去重，职业技能标签放在末尾
     # 先去重基础标签，保持原有顺序
     seen = set()
     unique_base = [x for x in base_tags if not (x in seen or seen.add(x))]
     # 添加职业技能标签（如果不在基础标签中）
     all_tags = unique_base + [s for s in skill_tags if s not in seen]
     if skill_tags:
         lprint(f'[标签合并] base={base_tags} + skill={skill_tags} = {all_tags}')

     return all_tags, matched_key

import re, json

# 读取文件
with open("trace.md", "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    content = f.read()

# 提取 JSON 索引
match = re.search(r'<<<JSON_INDEX>>>\s*```json\s*\n(.*?)\n```', content, re.DOTALL)
if match:
    data = json.loads(match.group(1))
    print(f"版本: {data['version']}")
    print(f"总调用: {data['metadata']['total_calls']}")
    print(f"最大深度: {data['metadata']['max_depth']}")
